Nantong 97

Provincial Order to Strictly Guard Against Banditry in Northern Jiangsu. The provincial government, noting the rampant banditry in northern Jiangsu counties and the cover provided by the burgeoning crops, issued a special order to the county heads of Tong, Rugao, Hai'an, and Taixing to jointly strengthen defense measures.

Dispute Over Education Funds Deposited as Collateral. Educational public funds in Nantong are deposited with merchants as collateral to generate interest. A fierce dispute has arisen between the education bureau and the merchants over the conversion rate between cash and silver dollars. Recently, the education bureau petitioned the county government, requesting prompt settlement based on the Judicial Yuan's interpretation, which stipulates that the silver dollar value should be based on the market price at the time of deposit. The merchants, however, argued that there were precedents in other counties of the province for resolving cash and silver dollar issues and were unwilling to accept the losses. The resolution remains uncertain.

County Government Reviews Case of Bandit Leader from Tong and Rugao. On the 18th, the Nantong County government reviewed the case of Feng Chensi, a bandit leader from Tong and Rugao. Feng's mother, Feng Jinshi, who had appealed to the provincial government, was also summoned for questioning. Feng, unable to deny the seizure of thirteen firearms and the testimonies of other bandits, offered no defense. His mother also provided little information. County Head Zhang plans to submit the case to the provincial government with a recommendation for the death penalty.

Pinghu 98

Another Highway Robbery in the City. Yao Yiquan, residing in Huitong, was robbed of 300 silver dollars by thugs last month, and the case remains unsolved. Yesterday afternoon (the 17th), Gu Zhizheng, who runs a scissors shop in the west of the county, had collected 50 silver dollars. While passing through Dongshijie Street inside the North Temple, he was attacked by six thugs who beat him severely and made off with all the money. Gu fought back, managing to grab one of the robbers. The other thugs pulled out knives, and Gu cried for help. Hearing the commotion, local residents rushed to the scene, causing the thugs to scatter. The apprehended robber was handed over to the Public Security Bureau, where clerk Yang interrogated him. The robber identified himself as Liu Chenglong, a former member of the anti-smuggling patrol, claiming he was acting on someone else's orders. He has been transferred to the county government for legal proceedings.

Police Assault Women. A man surnamed Zheng, a native of Pinghu, serves in the Shanghai Public Security Bureau. A few days ago, he returned to Pinghu from Shanghai and stayed at an inn in the east gate. The previous evening, Zheng took his wife out of the city, but the guards refused to open the gate, leading to a confrontation. Bystanders, feeling the injustice, slapped the guard twice. As a result, all were taken to the County Public Security Bureau. After questioning by Chief Huang, they were lightly reprimanded and released. Unexpectedly, upon returning to the entrance of Sangyuan Alley, they were attacked by several thugs, two of whom were wearing police uniforms. They were beaten severely, and knives were drawn. Merchants in the east gate area, thinking there was a fire, rushed out in alarm. Husband Takes Concubine, Mother and Daughter Commit Suicide. This spring, Yu took Jin Su'e, a woman from Wuxi, as a concubine in Shanghai and brought her home to live with his wife last month. At noon, a neighbor visited and, upon entering the room and discovering their condition, realized they had taken poison. Instigated by his stepmother, Huang became enraged and dragged and beat his daughter, striking her head with a wooden stick, causing a fatal injury to her temple. The case was transferred to the Hangzhou District Court for investigation. He was prosecuted for causing death by assault. Yesterday (the 18th), after questioning by judge Chen Luzhi of the criminal court, the court ruled that while Wang had the intention to harm, he did not intend to kill his own daughter, which was a mitigating factor. His sentence was reduced by one-half, and he was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment.

Educational News

Special Article 102

How Should Students Utilize Their Summer Vacation? By Liu Zhan'en.

The summer vacation is approaching, and schools nationwide are preparing to close and conclude the academic year. However, judging from past experiences, the majority of students tend to indulge in unrestricted play and unrestrained appetites during the summer vacation, leading to fatigue, illness, and a failure to grasp the meaning of the summer vacation and make good use of it.

During the summer vacation, students should still cherish their time, strive for moral development, cultivate and train their bodies, and engage with society and research. Subjects that cannot be researched during normal times should be pursued during this vacation. Students should not spend their days in idleness and indulgence, engaging in useless or harmful activities.

This year's summer vacation presents a different environment from previous years. Domestically, the flood disaster has not yet been recovered from, and externally, there is the pressure of powerful enemies. The landscape of the Northeast has changed color, and the scars of Shanghai are still fresh. At this critical moment of national crisis, students, as the backbone of the country's future, must work diligently, actively seek knowledge, and cultivate the strength to fight. They have no time for vacation. Therefore, in addition to ordinary summer vacation activities, they should utilize the summer vacation to engage in national salvation efforts, such as (1) implementing mass education, (2) promoting domestic goods, (3) participating in social improvement initiatives, and (4) advocating for the cessation of internal wars and the vigorous construction of a united front against foreign enemies. These are all areas where they can exert their efforts.

Currently, the *Shen Bao* is sponsoring an essay contest with prizes to guide students in utilizing their summer vacation. The topics emphasize practice, and students of all levels, from elementary to university, are eligible to participate. This method of encouraging young people has significant educational implications. It is hoped that school authorities and parents nationwide will encourage their children to participate so that young people across the country can understand the utilization of the summer vacation.

Over Twenty Experts from Other Locations Have Replied Confirming Attendance.

The Ministry of Education plans to hold a chemistry discussion meeting during the summer vacation, from August 1st to 7th. The Northwest Development Association has sent a letter requesting permission to participate, and a reply has been sent welcoming them. The main topics of discussion at this meeting will be the curriculum standards and translation of terms for applied chemistry. The meeting will first be divided into groups for discussion and then submitted to the general assembly for a public vote.

Local News

Details of Western Teacher Beating Students at Huatong Public School. 104

Poor Tea Snacks Lead to Physical Assault. On the 13th of this month, students of the Huatong Public School, established by the Shanghai Municipal Council in the Public Concession, requested newspapers to reveal the news of Mr. Auslice, the Western teacher, and Moffst, the principal, kicking and beating Hong Zuxiu, a student in the second grade of junior high school, and He Shengchang, a student in the third grade of middle school. Later, a reporter visited someone who had worked at the school, who said that every year as the summer vacation approached, the school held an academic exhibition and invited parents to a tea party. After the tea snacks, the principal would give a speech. The snacks prepared in previous years were palatable, but this year it was the opposite. Parents and students received only a paper bag of snacks containing a few pieces of coarse biscuits and cheap bread. The students were quite dissatisfied and blew up the paper bags of snacks into empty bags, making a popping sound. As a result, paper scraps flew everywhere. The Western teacher, Auslice, saw this and disliked it, ordering the students to pick them up and put them in the dustpan. Hong Zuxiu, a second-year student, stated that it was not his doing and explained the reason to the Western teacher, saying, "Why force people to do tea servant work?" Who knew that the teacher would kick and beat Hong before he finished speaking.

Picking Up Paper Scraps Repeatedly Evolves into Physical Altercation. After the kicking and beating, the Western teacher still wanted Hong to obey. Hong had no choice but to bow his head and pick up the paper scraps, placing them in the dustpan. The Western teacher repeatedly forced him to pick them up again and again. Hong could no longer endure it and threw the collected paper pieces back on the ground. The Western teacher considered this act an insult to a teacher and dragged and beat Hong to the faculty room and confined him, imposing a heavy punishment. As a result, two to three hundred students felt injustice, believing that the day of the parents' meeting should be a joyous day. Unexpectedly, the Western teacher acted so wildly, treating the students worse than servants. The students immediately elected He Shengchang, a third-year student, as their representative to negotiate with the principal for his release.

Principal Angered, Slaps Student Representative. During the conversation between the student representative He Shengchang and the principal, there was some misunderstanding in the language. During the speech, He Shengchang said, "Auslice is too uncivilized." The principal, upon hearing the word "uncivilized," became enraged and slapped He Shengchang's cheek three or four times, causing his lips, teeth, and tongue to collide, resulting in injury and bleeding in his mouth. At that time, more than a hundred family members of the students were still waiting quietly at the school for news. The students requested that the parents reason with the principal, but in the end, the principal was too prejudiced and could not be persuaded. The enthusiastic parents' meeting ended unhappily. Each parent came with excitement and left in disappointment.

Tearing Up the Northeast Map. It is also true that the principal tore up the Northeast map and the table of lost territories over the years. On the 13th, when the parents' meeting was held, the students' achievements were also displayed. A map of the three northeastern provinces and a table of lost territories over the years, made under the supervision of the Chinese teachers, were torn up by the principal. The Chinese teachers questioned this, and the principal apologized verbally for the loss of the map. The students were extremely angry and immediately posted anti-Japanese slogans. If they were torn up again, they planned to post slogans such as "Down with Imperialism" all over the school. Fortunately, the Western teachers were not familiar with Chinese and avoided a disturbance. However, the students were not happy, feeling that this was intolerable. The students of the school run by the Municipal Council, who had always been willing to obey, suddenly refused to pick up the pieces of paper, and there was a reason for it.

This is What the Head of Chinese and Western Education Said. On the 14th, the reporter visited Chen Heqin, the head of the Chinese Education Department of the Municipal Council. He said that he had not fully understood the Huatong Public School incident and had only learned some of the situation from the newspapers. The reporter then went to visit Mr. Hiller, the head of the Education Department of the Municipal Council, but Hiller had taken leave to return to his country. Mr. Komp, the former principal of Huatong Public School, was now acting as his replacement. The reporter visited under the name of an individual, but Komp was out. The next day (the 15th), the reporter inquired about the Huatong Public School incident by telephone, and he said that the Western teachers hated the students' disobedience, which led to the beating of the students. The school had begun its summer vacation on the 15th, and the school was very peaceful and there was nothing happening.

Male Teacher Had Not Finished Beating, Female Teacher Also Beat. The reporter went to Fanhuangdu again and met Ou Kui'an, a member of the Education Committee of the Municipal Council. Ou expressed surprise at this matter. He said that he himself was investigating the facts. On the 17th, the reporter went to Penglu and met He Zusheng, the student who was beaten. He said much the same as someone from the school's administration. He added that on that day, students had gathered on the lawn. The school authorities sent several Western teachers to guard the main routes in front of the principal's office, preventing the students from passing through. However, the lavatories had to be accessed by going past the principal's office. A student who was in urgent need of urination was blocked. He was beaten by Miss Moore, a Western teacher.

Students Request Assistance from Taxpayers' Association. Huatong Public School is now on holiday. After being beaten, the students requested assistance from the Chinese Taxpayers' Association.

World Olympic Games 112

Talk by Marathon King Nurmi

(Dentsu, Los Angeles, 18th) World marathon king, Finnish Paavo Nurmi, showed his brave figure at 3 p.m. today at the Olympic indoor stadium and immediately began practicing. After a short 30-minute break, a Dentsu reporter asked him, "How will the competition be this year?" He replied, "Normal. But I plan to shorten the record even more than the previous Amsterdam Games, but this is only regarding the marathon." (Question) "Does what you just said mean you have a very good chance of winning?" (Answer) "That is another question. Your country's Tsuda and Kwon Kim are formidable rivals. Argentina's Zabala and Germany's Teplow, like newly emerging comets, should not be underestimated." (Question) "Although the world expects it, we still believe you can win the championship." (Answer) "I will work hard. I also wish your country's athletes good luck."

American Newspaper Predicts Japan May Rank Third 113

(Dentsu, Los Angeles, 18th) With only ten days left until the start of the Games, Japanese track and field athletes are training more intensely. Track and field stars Oda, Nambu, Yoshioka, Nishida, etc., have adapted to the foreign environment, and new records are gradually appearing. However, the Japanese coaching staff has not released the daily records due to strategic considerations. Detectives from various countries are constantly lurking, specifically seeking information. Sports reporters from American newspapers are also detectives. They secretly watched Yoshioka's 10.4-second 100-meter practice time with astonishment, saying he is as strong as [illegible]. American newspapers published prediction articles stating that Japan may rank third in the Games. Japanese head coach Yamamoto recognizes this criticism as a public assessment.

Second Batch of Japanese Athletes Arrive in Los Angeles 114

Dentsu, Los Angeles, 18th. The Taiyo Maru, carrying the second batch of Japanese athletes sent to attend the Olympics, arrived at San Pedro at 10 a.m. today. Olympic officials and Japanese people in Los Angeles gave a special welcome. The ship raised the Japanese flag and sailed to the harbor to greet them. After disembarking, the athletes boarded dozens of cars, with a music band car leading the procession for more than 30 miles, accompanied by welcoming Japanese people. They arrived in Los Angeles at 11 a.m. There, they were welcomed everywhere. In particular, the Japanese female athletes attracted the attention of the people of Los Angeles. The athletes then went to Los Angeles City Hall for a welcome reception before parading through the Japanese quarter. The female athletes went to the Chapman Park Hotel, while the male athletes went to the Olympic Village.

On School Physical Education (II) Lu Xiangqian 115

(3) Training Overly Emphasizes Athletes, Opportunities Are Not Equal. A school's physical education director or teacher, today, who painstakingly seeks to popularize physical education throughout the school, or train in health methods, is not only dismissed as [illegible] by ordinary people, but even students will regard them as mediocre and incompetent. Most people view physical education directors and teachers only as those who can connect with athletes, or lead athletes to expeditions to certain places at certain times, as their supreme authority. Physical education directors or teachers only say, "So-and-so is a national sprint champion, so-and-so is a soccer star and basketball player. In such-and-such year, month, and day, I led them to participate in a certain competition and win a certain championship. All of this was developed through my training, and they are all my talented students." They are invariably proud, as if overwhelmed with glory. They do not know that driving people to fight, creating a lack of specialization in studies, and the pain of having nowhere to turn after graduation are all caused by these so-called directors and professors. Furthermore, considering the many students who gradually develop hunchbacks or even die young from lung disease due to the lack of appropriate physical training and sports opportunities, it is not enough. As a physical education director or teacher, do they not recognize this as their responsibility, and do they not feel ashamed and guilty? Over the years, seeing the overemphasis on training by general school physical education directors and teachers, and the inequality of sports and health opportunities for most people, I deeply regret it. In the future, I hope that those who are directors or teachers, as well as athletes and non-athletes, should all have a deep understanding and clarity of their own rights and obligations. Then, it will be close to the ideal. (Athlete sports are not inappropriate to promote, but should not become a special class.)

(4) Advocating Mass Sports Requires Popularization Among the Common People. The failure of school authorities and those in charge of sports administration to advocate physical education has already been discussed above. Now, at a time when the country is in trouble and the economy is declining, it is especially important to adapt to the times and advocate for the whole country, striving for popularization and accessibility to the common people, so that most people can get physical training and health opportunities. Schools are the starting point. From schools, it should be extended to society, so that all our people, regardless of gender, age, get physical and health training. Then the nation can be strong, and national humiliation can be wiped out. Looking at the errors in past methods of promoting school physical education, the failure to enable the masses to share exercise opportunities is indeed a major cause of today's national weakness. However, most of those who advocate school physical education are still stuck in the imitation of accumulated habits, believing that having a large soccer field, a vast cinder track, and well-equipped tennis courts, as well as foreign sports equipment costing dozens of gold coins, is sufficient to promote physical education. This erroneous concept is a major obstacle to physical education. Today's schools, not only do general students think this way, but also general trendy physical education directors or teachers think this way. Ask the schools across the country, how many have such economic capacity and equipment? Even if they do, ask Shanghai after the January 28th Incident, once the schools themselves are reduced to war zones, most schools plan to relocate, taking classes in narrow alleys and small rooms. Ask yourself, under these circumstances, with the place already feeling small and the economy feeling difficult, as a physical education director or teacher, can you still rely on spacious fields and large buildings, holding volleyballs and basketballs to take the stage and implement your physical education policy? Or should you think of remedial measures, adapt to the environment, and work harder to promote it, not being bound by the current situation? This is a strategy and plan that should be planned by physical education directors or teachers in schools that have been reduced to war zones, as well as those who are preparing for unexpected disasters in the future. In my opinion, those responsible for physical education should usually advocate physical education that is popular and accessible to students. Popularization means not necessarily having a large sports field and perfect and expensive equipment, while still being able to get sports and exercise opportunities. That is, being able to exercise the body and improve health anytime, anywhere, which is conducive to the environment and a method of promotion that is not influenced by the environment. Accessibility means that everyone can get easy and simple sports opportunities and methods, not being困by the economy, and not being limited by techniques. By promoting school physical education in this way, and extending it to social physical education, it will be easy, simple, and most universal. (The End)

Although there were ups and downs afterward, it remained around 751 liang for the longest time, probably because there were no special changes in foreign exchange. Later, the market seemed firm, but the premium was only slightly more than one liang. Later, it was calculated to be about 53 liang. In August, 400 to 500 bars were dropped, and the shorts still paid out 2 liang and 2 qian. Now, Wing Fung, Hang Seng, Dalian Bang, Tai Cheong, and others are swapping. Liaodong Self-Defense Army Cables for Assistance Yesterday 134

Saving the Northeast is Saving China

Hoping All Compatriots Across the Nation Will Rise Up and Respond

Tang Juyu, Commander-in-Chief of the Liaodong Self-Defense Army, cabled the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "The country is unfortunate, and the Japanese invaders are encroaching, seizing our land, slaughtering our people, coercing the Han people, and establishing a puppet state. Their various atrocities are beyond description. Juyu and others mourn the disintegration of our land, grieve for the refugees, and vow to defend against disaster with a bleeding heart. We have secretly entered Liaodong and contacted comrades. In a matter of months, followers are like clouds. Thus, on the horse day of April, we swore an oath with blood, and delivered a speech with tears. At the same time, fourteen counties raised the banner of righteousness. Soldiers and civilians were united, sharing a common hatred. Knowing that the masses are no match for the few, and that the strengths are disparate, but in order to fight for the survival of the country and the personality of the nation, any sacrifice is acceptable. In the past two or three months, in Liuhe, Lingjie, Kuandian, Chuanmutai, Yongdianling, Waikekou, Linjiang, and other places, there have been dozens of battles of all sizes. We fought with Chen Bing, pulled flags, and fought to climb. We only mark with red blood, and we do not resign from stepping on sharp blades. The morale of the soldiers is strong, and the Japanese invaders are terrified. However, the lone army is isolated, and there is a shortage of supplies and ammunition. Although there are plans to directly attack Shenyang in three routes, it is difficult to achieve them as scheduled. When I touched my heart at night, I felt deeply ashamed. Now, when the green gauze screen rises and the weeds grow, it is the time for the Japanese invaders and us to fight for the final victory. They are increasing the transfer of elite troops, and the oppression against us is increasing. If it lasts for a long time, I am afraid that we will eventually be taken advantage of by the enemy. Juyu swears to dedicate himself to the country and has long placed life and death out of consideration. What I cannot bear to ignore is the suffering of my 14 counties in Liaodong. When I think of this, I have no tears to shed. In short, saving Liaodong is saving the Northeast, and saving the Northeast is saving China. The situation is urgent, and there is no time to lose. I hope that all compatriots across the country will be aware of the difficulties and dangers, and rise up and respond urgently, so that the merits of several months will not be wasted in one day. The cable is urgent, and I am greatly looking forward to it. Tang Juyu, Commander-in-Chief of the Liaodong People's Self-Defense Army, led Huang Yuzhou, Wang Yuwen, Zhang Weidong, Ying Ruoyu, Zhang Zongguo, Tang Yuzhen, Lin Zhenhuai, Chang Yongan, Deng Tiemei, Li Chunrun, Sun Xiu, Xu Dasan, Li Tanglin, Guo Jingzhi, Wang Xiangbin, Wen Dianjia, Zheng Yufeng, Tan Guanghai, Sun Gengjiu, and all the generals and soldiers respectfully knock their heads, Han."

Customs Authorities Discussed Counter-Locking Liaoguan Yesterday 135

The Japanese Government's Second Reply Can Be Sent Out Soon

The Government Authorities Decided to Implement a Counter-Locking Policy

Regarding the Northeast customs issue, after the Ministry of Foreign Affairs lodged its second protest with Japan, the Japanese side ignored the views of the government authorities and decided to implement counter-locking when necessary, regardless of whether it responded or not. However, during the transitional period before counter-locking is implemented, there have been recent discoveries of many goods transported from the Northeast to the mainland that hold counterfeit tax receipts from the puppet state. The authorities formally studied the countermeasures yesterday. The news is divided into the following:

Japanese Attitude Yesterday, according to the secretary of the Japanese Embassy, ​​Okazaki, to the reporter of the Xinsheng News Agency, the Central Government's second protest against the Northeast customs issue had already been received. The Japanese government's prepared reply will be sent out soon. The content is roughly the same as the last reply from the Chinese government, stating that the seizure of the Chinese customs in Northeast China has nothing to do with the Japanese government, and the change of the Dalian tax collector is a violation of the agreement, it is said.

Counter-locking Liaoguan Yesterday it was heard that the resolution of the Northeast customs issue has not yet reached the stage of a formal international conference, and is being directly negotiated between China and Japan. However, the Japanese side only accepted the protest against the Dalian customs incident and resigned from other responsibilities. Our authorities have now decided that regardless of their reply or even ignoring it, they will implement counter-locking of Northeast customs when necessary.

Transitional Measures According to diplomatic circles, after receiving a certain document from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the customs authorities a few days ago, the customs authorities in this port held a meeting at about 10:00 a.m. yesterday, led by Zhang Fuyun, Director of the Customs Administration, together with representatives of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance, to study the transitional measures before implementing counter-locking of Northeast customs. This is because recently, the mainland has successively discovered goods transported from the Northeast. Whether to allow them to be unloaded or to collect the export tax from the other side on their behalf are all urgent tasks. As a result, because the authorities strictly maintained secrecy, it is still unknown at present.

British Government's Attitude Towards the Puppet State 136

The London dispatch of the Zilin News on the 18th stated, "The reporter can assert that the British Foreign Office now recognizes that if Japan recognizes Manchuria at this time, it will be an extremely provocative act, easily inviting criticism from all parties. The attitude of the British government is to firmly adhere to the Washington Nine-Power Treaty of 1922, especially with regard to the recognized territorial integrity of China in that treaty. Furthermore, the League of Nations investigation team will send out its investigation report at the end of September. Before this report is sent to the League of Nations, any action that may hinder the territorial integrity of China is of course not welcomed by the British government. However, at the same time, it also gives a sympathetic observation to the current administration of Manchuria, and it is willing to give it de facto recognition at an appropriate time in the future, it is said."

Memorial Hall for Mr. Yingshi Held an Opening Ceremony Yesterday 137

More than 500 People Attended

The Ceremony Was Exceptionally Grand

The Memorial Hall for the revolutionary martyr Mr. Chen Gong Yingshi was initiated by the members of the Lake Society. Construction began in May of the 18th year and was approved by the central government. It was built on the original site of Chansheng Temple at the corner of Guizhou Road and Beijing Road. In the middle, the construction was suspended due to the Shanghai Incident, so it was postponed until yesterday morning before the completion and opening ceremony was held.

The Thoughtful Reception Before the opening, Chen Aishi, the director of the Lake Society, personally went to the site to take care of and arrange everything, which was extremely meticulous. He also sent a letter to the police, asking them to send police to direct traffic in front of the house. It is estimated that about 30 Chinese and Western Indian detectives were sent, and the Moor Hall Boy Scouts were stationed inside to maintain order. Chen Aishi also personally led the executive committee to receive guests in the hall, and politely refused those who did not wear badges to avoid congestion.

A Glimpse of the Venue On the gate of the Lake Society, the national party flag emblem was hung, and it was fully decorated with green pines and colorful flowers. On both sides of the entrance were the signature areas. The front was a white Italian stone staircase with carved railings on both sides, which was very beautiful. The second floor was the main hall of the Memorial Hall. The site was wide and the light was sufficient. The patterns on the four walls were made of light yellow, lake color, and plain white. It was quiet and beautiful, and the plaques donated by various circles were fully hung around. The center was the podium, and the middle was the chairman's table, which was equipped with a microphone. On both sides were piles of flowers and flower baskets donated by the Central Party Department, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Military Affairs Commission, and Lin Chairman, Chiang Chairman, Wang President, He Yingqin, Wu Tiecheng, and other important figures. After the curtain was opened, a Party emblem made of fresh flowers on a wall full of green pines was seen. In the middle was the portrait of President Sun Yat-sen, and below it was the military uniform portrait of Mr. Yingshi, with fresh flowers and colored lights decorating the mirror frame around. The seats on both sides of the platform were for representatives, and the seats in the hall were spacious. Before 9:00, the representatives and guests from all parties who participated were crowded. The third floor was the building box of the Memorial Hall. The left ear box was the seat for the military band, the right ear box was the seat for the ambulance team, and the front box was the seat for reporters.

Solemn Opening Ceremony: Yesterday morning at 9:20, the meeting was opened with a bell. Shen Tianxin presided over the ceremony. (1) Everyone stood at attention. (2) The presidium, consisting of Wu Tiecheng, Shao Yuan Chong, He Yingqin, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Chu Fucheng, Chen Qinshi, and Chen Aishi, took their seats amidst the music of the Public Security Bureau Military Band. (3) Wu Tiecheng, representing the Central Government, performed the unveiling ceremony. (4) Music was played. (5) The Party anthem was sung. (6) The most respectful salute was given to the Party and national flags and the portrait of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. (7) The Chairman respectfully read Premier Sun's will and presented flowers. (8) Memorial texts from the Central Party Headquarters, Military Affairs Commission, Ministry of Military Affairs, Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, and Lake Society were read aloud. (9) Chairman Wu Tiecheng delivered a speech. (10) Chen Qicai, Chairman of the Lake Society, reported on the process of building the memorial hall. (11) Shao Yuan Chong reported on the life and deeds of Chen Gongying Shi. (12) He Yingqin, Ye Chucang, Wang Xiaolai, Zhuang Songfu, Wen Yinxing (representing Huang Fu), Tao Baichuan (representing the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters), Zhang Zhongdao (representing the Nanjing Municipal Party Headquarters), and Zheng Zhengqiu gave speeches. (13) Chen Qinshi, representing the Chen family, delivered a thank-you speech. (14) A photograph was taken. (15) The ceremony concluded.

Wu Tiecheng's Speech: Today is the completion ceremony of Mr. Chen Ying Shi's Memorial Hall. Mr. Ying Shi's contributions were for the good of the Party and the nation. His great achievements and noble spirit have great significance not only in China's past history, but also in the future of the country and society. Today, the government authorities, members of the Lake Society, and the citizens of Shanghai, based on this purpose, built this hall, not only to commemorate Mr. Chen but also to promote Mr. Chen's spirit to alert the people. Today, our country is still in turmoil, and social undertakings are mostly undeveloped. It is hoped that the people will continue Mr. Chen's spirit, work hard and strive to consolidate the foundation of the country, and promote social undertakings. Then the meaning of building this hall can be said to be not obliterated.

Chen Qicai's Report: Chen Qicai, Chairman of the Lake Society, reported on the construction of the Ying Shi Memorial Hall, saying: In the sixteenth year of the Republic [1927], the National Revolutionary Army established itself in the Southeast. The Society commemorated Mr. Ying Shi's revolutionary achievements and submitted a report to the National Government, requesting that a memorial be built for Mr. Ying Shi to show respect and appreciation. At that time, the planned construction included four items: a memorial hall, a business school, a park, and a library. At that time, the Society was preparing to build its own premises, raising funds and looking for land, and actively proceeding. In May of the eighteenth year of the Republic [1929], a report was submitted to the National Government, which ordered the establishment of the Martyr Chen Gong Ying Shi Memorial Hall within the Shanghai Lake Society premises and allocated 50,000 national currency. Subsequently, the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Shanghai Municipal Government allocated 20,000 national currency each, and the Zhejiang Provincial Government allocated 30,000 provincial public bonds, all to subsidize the construction costs of the memorial hall. The Society successively claimed these funds and respectfully hired workers to build the hall. By this month, the project was completed. The construction costs were barely met. Although the internal furnishings and equipment still need to be raised separately, the opening ceremony is being held today, and the various facilities are not yet complete. Please forgive us.

He Yingqin's Speech: Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin said in his speech, "Today is the opening day of the Chen Ying Shi Memorial Hall. I also have the opportunity to come and participate in this grand ceremony, which is a great honor. Regarding Mr. Ying Shi's past efforts in the revolution and his personal thoughts and character, all those who admire him must have a considerable understanding, and there is no need for me to narrate them in detail. However, as we face the many difficulties and tribulations of the country today, with the Red bandits rampant internally, poisoning several provinces, and the Japanese invading externally, forcibly occupying the Northeast, and as we come to Shanghai, which was once bombed and destroyed by Japanese aircraft and warships, to commemorate Mr. Chen, who sacrificed for the revolution more than ten years ago, we see Mr. Chen's spirit of courage, perseverance, and refusal to give up, and we feel more keenly the importance and magnitude of the revolutionary responsibility in the future. We can only hope that the comrades of our Party and the people of the whole country will unite in sincerity and work together to shoulder this important and great revolutionary responsibility, so that the Chinese nation can embark on the path of freedom and equality. Mr. Ying Shi once said to people, 'I hate power and like to fight injustice most in my life. Whenever I see things where the strong bully the weak, I must be angry and feel injustice. Now the world is still an unfair world, so I am willing to do the work of world revolution. However, China now needs revolution as soon as possible. I am also Chinese, so I will start with the Chinese revolution first. After the Chinese revolution is successful, I will do my best to help the revolution of all weak countries and the people of perished countries, so that the power in the world can be completely eliminated, and all nations in the world can achieve independence and freedom. My wish may be completely achieved.' Mr. Ying Shi was killed on May 18th of the fifth year of the Republic [1916]. Although he was envied by Yuan Shikai, his ambition to not see the success of the Chinese National Revolution and to fulfill his great ambition of world harmony was not realized, but his great spirit of saving China and saving mankind is worthy of our admiration and emulation. Now Japan is bullying China everywhere, disregarding all international peace treaties, and no one in the international community has ever upheld justice and imposed severe sanctions on the violent. The so-called independence and freedom of all nations in the world is really far from being achieved. Now we want to commemorate Mr. Chen, and we should follow Mr. Chen's spirit of courage, perseverance, adventure, progress, and struggle, and hold on to a long-term and continuous resistance to the Japanese violent and unreasonable invasion, so that power is eliminated and justice is upheld. Only then can the Chinese nation be liberated by itself, and then can it do its best to help the nations of all weak countries and perished countries and seek mutual liberation. Moreover, the harm of the Red bandits is worse than that of ferocious beasts and floods. In recent years, they have taken advantage of opportunities to obstruct the progress of the National Revolution. This year's war of resistance against Japan has been particularly affected by them. Now we want to commemorate Mr. Chen and complete Mr. Chen's work of striving for the Chinese National Revolution and then striving for world harmony. In particular, we should unite the whole country and concentrate our strength to fundamentally eliminate the Red bandits, so that the National Revolution can have no worries, and its united front against foreign enemies can be consolidated. Mr. Ying Shi also often said to people, 'Opportunities must be created and cannot be waited for. If we can work hard to create opportunities, then even if we cannot sit and wait for success ourselves, we can also create a big trend to promote the progress of society.' Mr. Ying Shi was a revolutionary practitioner. Although he failed many times, he still moved forward constantly, never hesitating and waiting for the revolution to come by itself. Today, the Chinese National Revolution is able to have this foundation, which is naturally created by the Premier's great spirit and personality. However, Mr. Ying Shi faithfully obeyed the Premier's doctrines and actively assisted the revolution. Although he could not succeed, he has already achieved martyrdom. Today, in the newly completed memorial hall, we commemorate him. It is best for everyone to remember these last words firmly, follow them earnestly, and it will definitely be of great help to the success of the National Revolution."

Ye Chucang's Speech: In this magnificent venue, commemorating the bright and great Mr. Chen Ying Shi, we can get an idea that brightness comes from hardship. At this time when the country is in trouble, today in this magnificent memorial hall, reporting on Mr. Ying Shi's history and praising Mr. Ying Shi's personality, we must also know Mr. Ying Shi's former hardships. In the past, ordinary people had roads to walk, but Mr. Ying Shi had no roads to walk. Ordinary people had houses to live in, but Mr. Ying Shi had no houses to live in. Almost under the power of the reactionary warlords, there was no place for Mr. Ying Shi to stand. In the past, Mr. Ying Shi lived in a small building in Yuyang Lane, planning the national military and political affairs. This magnificent memorial hall came from that small building that was not tolerated by others. Here, we can prove that brightness comes from hardship. Now, difficulties have come again, and they are ten or a hundred times greater than the difficulties that Mr. Ying Shi felt at that time. So, how are we going to find brightness from hardship again? We know that we cannot learn from Mr. Ying Shi now, but we still have to learn from Mr. Ying Shi, that is, to learn from Mr. Ying Shi to find brightness from hardship.

Wang Xiaolai's Speech: Mr. Chen Ying Shi's revolutionary spirit is admired by the people of the whole country. I was originally a friend of Mr. Ying Shi and followed Mr. Chen, so I saw Mr. Chen's great spirit. Mr. Chen was taciturn, doing what he said, without hesitation. Therefore, his discussions were few and his successes were many. Mr. Chen not only worked hard for the country, but also benefited farmers, industry, and commerce. For example, the fact that the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce has such a great venue at Tianhougong Bridge today is also due to Mr. Chen's assistance during the era of the Shanghai Military Governor. Today, you commemorate Mr. Chen, and you should not forget the revolutionary spirit that Mr. Chen left behind. In the future, anyone who dares to engage in civil war is not worthy of Mr. Ying Shi. Anyone who cannot unite against foreign enemies is not worthy of Mr. Ying Shi. Anyone who does not promote national goods is not worthy of Mr. Ying Shi. We must unite our spirits and resist foreign insults together so that we will not fail the meaning of commemorating Mr. Chen today.

Japanese Troops and Japanese Side Have No Intention of Withdrawing from the Gongda and Toyota Factories 139

Headquarters of the Naval Landing Force Issued a Statement Yesterday

Dagong News Agency reports: After the Japanese troops in District D completely withdrew, our side believes that several dozen Japanese naval and army soldiers are still stationed at the Gongda Yarn Factory in Yinxiang Township and the Toyota Yarn Factory in Caojiadu and have not yet withdrawn. This cannot be said to be a complete restoration to the original state before January 28th. Our side, Yu Hongjun, has negotiated with Mr. Okazaki, a Japanese commissioner, several times, requesting withdrawal, but there has been no result. The headquarters of the Japanese Special Naval Landing Force issued a statement specifically on this matter yesterday, expressing no intention of withdrawing. The statement roughly stated that after the withdrawal of troops stationed in District D, the Chinese authorities believed that the Japanese naval and army soldiers still stationed at the Gongda and Toyota yarn factories were not satisfactory and insisted on withdrawal, which was a misunderstanding. It was found that troops have always been stationed at the two factories for protection, which was the case before the January 28th Incident and was absolutely unrelated to the Shanghai war. Therefore, the withdrawal of troops stationed in District D this time is not bound by the ceasefire agreement signed on May 5th. Moreover, the stationed troops are purely for the protection of the yarn factories and do not hinder local security. The Chinese authorities cannot use this as an excuse. However, the headquarters of the Naval Landing Force believes that it will soon be able to automatically withdraw the troops stationed at the two factories within an appropriate period of time.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Plans to Formulate Measures for the Disposal of Existing Japanese Goods 140

Yesterday, It Sent a Letter to All Trade Associations for Notification

Dagong News Agency reports: The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday formulated measures for the disposal of existing Japanese goods and sent a letter to all trade associations, stating: "Dear Sirs, on the 19th of May, fifteen trade associations, including the Cotton Cloth Industry, Color Printing Industry, Brick and Ash Industry, Mineral Ash Factory, Lime Sales Industry, Intestine Industry, Gunny Sack Industry, Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry, Silk and Satin Industry, Yarn Industry, Floss Industry, Ginseng and Bird's Nest Industry, Sugar Industry, Coal Industry, and Electrical Appliance Industry, stated in a letter that since the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association stopped working, there have been no measures for the disposal of existing goods. However, it was found that although these goods are inferior goods, they were all purchased by our people with sweat and blood before the Shenyang Incident [Mukden Incident]. If appropriate solutions are not sought, not only will merchants suffer huge losses, but also the social economy will be endangered, which will not help the enemy country. Recently, it was heard that the municipal government is dealing with the unfinished cases of the Anti-Japanese Association, so it is necessary to properly formulate appropriate disposal measures for the goods previously stored by various industries to seek relief and prevent abuses. However, the organizations of various industries are different, and the environments are also different. If a simple method is used universally, it is inevitable that the disease of cutting the feet to fit the shoes will occur. The various trade associations have closer relations with their members and have more relevant knowledge. If your association is responsible for each trade association to separately formulate disposal measures with the principle of preventing abuses, and strictly urge all members to never buy or sell Japanese goods again, it will be more effective and convenient. Therefore, we jointly request that you grant approval, which is in the public interest, etc.' After the meeting, it was decided that each industry should formulate and report appropriate solutions for the existing Japanese goods, depending on the situation, for adoption and implementation, to seek relief and prevent abuses. After the meeting, nine industries responded, and the methods formulated by the Taxi Industry Association and the Cotton Cloth Industry Association were the most practical and detailed. Although the other industries advocated different degrees of detail, they agreed that the associations should be responsible.

Page 14

"Associations should be responsible for checking the source of goods in and out, to prevent the continuation of Japanese goods privately. Distribute a volunteer letter and ask each store to fill in the form themselves, and after that never import Japanese goods. Then, the association can organize a group to check and punish stores that import Japanese goods privately." The general idea is the same, which shows that the idea of never buying Japanese goods again has become a widespread and consistent proposition, and the patriotic sentiment of merchants has become more and more firm, which is admirable. It was submitted to the third regular meeting of the second session for discussion, and it was decided that the industries that have not yet responded to the measures for the disposal of existing Japanese goods should also follow the above methods and formulate them properly by each association, and strive to prevent abuses so that private individuals cannot take advantage of the situation. However, each industry must require its members to fill out a voluntary letter and resolutely not import Japanese goods in the future. The association should check at any time, and the above opinions of the regular meeting should be submitted to the second executive committee for discussion and approval on file. It was found that the Japanese aggression in the Eastern Provinces is becoming more and more obvious. Recently, it has openly declared to China and foreign countries that Manchuria will never be returned to China. It is an obvious fact that the Chinese nation must fight to the end against Japan in order to survive. The Northeast Volunteer Army, even in the most difficult circumstances, does not hesitate to sever their bellies and give their lives for the country. All Chinese people must sever economic relations with Japan to provide spiritual support for the Volunteer Army and to control the fate of the crazy enemy economically. Perhaps both sides can advance together, or there will be a day when they will repent and return our occupied land. Therefore, we have recorded the case and notified all associations, one side should pay attention to the disposal of deposited goods, so that they cannot take advantage of the situation, and the other side should pay attention to the prevention of Japanese goods in the future, so as not to cause a resurgence of ashes. In short, if the Chinese nation is not to fall, we must first seek the non-degeneration of our merchants. This huge responsibility, the association is willing to encourage each other with all the associations. Sincerely, and with blessings, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce."

The Dried and Preserved Goods Industry Plans to Resist Inferior Goods 141

Appointed Personnel to Be Responsible for Reporting

Dagong News Agency reports: The Dried and Preserved Goods Industry Trade Union of this city deeply regrets that just after the disaster of the January 28th Incident, treacherous merchants, driven by greed and lust, are openly selling inferior goods. The union found that the sales of inferior goods such as white sugar, dried scallops, salted seafood, agar, dried mushrooms, broken ends, seafood, etc. have been quite alarming recently, and effective methods should be used to stop them. Therefore, it was decided at a meeting yesterday to appoint Yu Yaoqiu, Yao Fenglin, Sun Chunshan, Hu Xiaoxiang, Ling Baode, Cheng Wenkui, Mei Lanqing and other seven people to be responsible for actively reporting treacherous merchants from now on, and three measures were formulated: (1) Publish the names of treacherous merchants in the newspaper; (2) Sprinkle stinky chemicals on all inferior goods; (3) Send a letter to the trade association to revoke their membership and revoke their market certificates.

The Import of Japanese Goods Has Increased Sharply 142

It Has Returned to the Top Import Position

After September 18th [Mukden Incident], the city established the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, and the boycott movement was carried out vigorously. The import of Japanese goods was greatly affected, and it dropped from the first position to the third position. British goods occupied the first position, and American goods occupied the second position. Unexpectedly, after the signing of the ceasefire agreement, the import of Japanese goods became active again, especially Japanese coal, Japanese sugar, and cotton textiles. It has now recovered from the third position to the first position. It is heard that all sectors of the city are now trying to discuss and take effective methods to curb this activity.

Japanese Naval Landing Force and Armored Vehicles Arrived in Shanghai 143

The Shanghai Japanese Naval Landing Force already has 2,500 men, and recently two more batches have been transferred, totaling 600 men. The first batch arrived in Shanghai first, and the second batch arrived yesterday afternoon.

The first batch of 250 naval landing force members arrived in Shanghai on the transport ship Noharu. Furthermore, the Japanese Ministry of the Navy transferred 350 naval group landing force members from the Sasebo Naval Port and transported them to Shanghai on the special service ship Qingdao. It was originally scheduled to enter the port at 5:00 AM, but due to the ebb tide, it was changed to 2:00 PM to arrive at Yangshupu and land at the Osaka Merchant Shipping Wharf.

An armored vehicle, named Patriotic No. 1, was donated by the people of Nagaoka, Japan, and was brought to Shanghai on the Qingdao Maru yesterday. It was originally intended to be unloaded today, but it has been changed to 4:00 PM today. The ship also unloaded a large number of guns, ammunition.

Yu Hongjun Visited Feixindun Yesterday to Discuss the Issue of Building Roads Beyond the Border 144

Verbal Refutation of the Points Raised by the Bureau of Public Works

Serious Declaration That Chinese Sovereignty Cannot Be Disregarded

The issue of building roads beyond the border has been delayed for more than a week since the special board meeting of the Bureau of Public Works on the sixth of this month, due to the illness of Feixindun, the Director-General of the Bureau of Public Works. Yu Hongjun, the representative of the municipal government, telegraphed Feixindun yesterday morning to inquire about how the issue was proceeding. Li Binrong, the design director of the Shanghai Northwest Minsheng Reclamation Company, has consulted with Hu many times and has sent a telegram to Shaanxi, ordering Zhang Lianquan of the Minsheng Company to inform Deng Xiaoshan to provide guidance and assistance when the inspection group arrives in Shaanxi.

Departure Route Information: The shipping bureau asked the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Industry to also send special personnel to join the group. It is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on July 25th, arrive in Zhengzhou on August 10th for assembly, and arrive in Xi'an on August 15th. Reception centers will be set up in Zhengzhou and Xi'an. The inspection period for the group members is scheduled for 35 days, and they will return to Xi'an on September 20th. Transportation, food, lodging, communication, hygiene, etc. along the way will be handled by the shipping bureau's general affairs and medical affairs offices.

North and South Route Inspection: After the group members arrive in Xi'an, they will be divided into north and south routes for inspection. The south route goes from Xi'an to the Qinling Mountains, passing through Xingping, Wugong, Fengxiang, Baoji, Jianchaping, Fengxian, Miaotaizi, Liuba, Zhong, Mianxian, Hanzhong, Chenggu, Xixiang, Shiquan, Hanyin, Ankang, Zhen'an, Xiaoyi, etc. The north route passes through Sanyuan, Dali, He County, Hancheng, Longmen, Jiyi Town, Yichuan, Yanchang, Fushi, Ganquan, Fu County, Luochuan, Zhongbu, Yijun, Tongguan, Yao County, and ends at Sanyuan.

Important Northwest Products: Important Northwest products include cotton from Xingping, coal, iron, and medicine from Fengxian, gold from Hanzhong, forests from Hanyin, placer gold from Nanzheng, lead from Xunyang, copper from Zhen'an, mercury from Lueyang, salt from Dali, jade from Lantian, and especially petroleum from Yanchang County, which is enough for the world to use for 300 years. Hancheng County alone has 100,000 tons of unexploited coal reserves. The central government has now sent petroleum expert Zhong Ying to the Northwest to test oil wells. Overseas Chinese also joined this inspection group, and Hu Shuhua is also paying attention to petroleum, saying that after the inspection, he plans to raise more than 10 million to open oil wells.

Important Notice for Money Exchanges Regarding Reserve Fund 147

Failure to Meet 60% Threshold Will Result in Refusal to Sign

Regarding the issue of abolishing the tael and adopting the yuan, since Xu Kan, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, came to Shanghai, a basic decision has been made. Minister of Finance Song Ziwen only needs to visit Shanghai again to discuss and finalize the legal tender price and silver content with the banking and money exchange sectors. The Ministry of Finance can then issue a formal decree to abolish the tael and adopt the yuan. The money exchange sector agrees with this principle in general, but is concerned that the abolition of the tael will be the only step taken, and there will be no good solution for the adoption of the yuan. Even more, they worry that today the yuan will be adopted, tomorrow the jiao will be changed, and the day after the copper coin will be changed, implementing it step by step, which will make it even more difficult to unify the currency system. A reporter from the Kuo Wen News Agency inquired from various parties yesterday and recorded the findings as follows:

Song and Xu Will Come Together: Minister of Finance Song Ziwen departed from Hankou for Lushan and is rumored to return to Beijing today. A reporter inquired at the Song residence yesterday and learned that Song's mission to Hankou included (1) military expenses and (2) tax matters, but also necessitated contacting various sectors in Hankou regarding the abolition of the tael and adoption of the yuan. As for the delay in Lushan, it was to meet with Chairman of the National Government Lin Sen. Now that Mr. Song is scheduled to return to Beijing today, he will likely come to Shanghai the day after tomorrow, and Xu Kan will also come to Shanghai together.

Money Exchange Provisional Meeting: The Money Exchange Association held a provisional meeting at the association the night before last. More than seventy managers of various money exchanges, including Qin Runqing, Yu Zuoting, and Li Shoushan, attended. After the meeting began, there was also a detailed discussion on the issue of abolishing the tael and adopting the yuan. It is reported that, to prevent a crisis in the credit of paper money, it was resolved: (1) to reorganize the Special Property Custody Committee, and its name will be changed to the Money Exchange Joint Reserve, with a total of 30 million, including 27 million in assets and 3 million in cash; (2) to telegraph to the association's representative examining the issuance reserve, stating that the implementation of abolishing the tael and using the yuan is not far off, and if the reserve cash is less than 60%, do not sign under any circumstances, to protect the safety of the social economy.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation and Guangdong Aviation Change Flight Route 151

From Guangdong via Shantou, Fujian, Ningbo, Hangzhou to Shanghai

Connecting with the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Hankou Line

The Eurasia Aviation Corporation is actively preparing the Hankou-Guangdong line. The originally planned route starts from Hankou, passes through Yuezhou, Changsha, Zhuzhou, Leiyang, Changle, Zhaoguan, and other stations to reach Guangzhou. However, according to a spokesman for the company yesterday, Eurasia Aviation Corporation is preparing the Hankou-Guangdong route for the convenience of domestic transportation, and not to compete with the China National Aviation Corporation in business. Therefore, it had informal consultations with the China National Aviation Corporation to change the route to go from Huangzhou via Shantou, Fuzhou, Ningbo, and Hangzhou to reach Shanghai, connecting with the company's Shanghai-Hankou route. Once the preparations are completed, it will arrange a test flight.

Sanyou Industrial Society's Retail Store Reopens Today 152

Result of Yesterday's Social Affairs Bureau Inquiry

Food Expenses Maintained by the Company as Usual

After the labor unrest occurred at the Sanyou Industrial Society factory in Yinxiang Township, the Nanjing Road retail store temporarily suspended business due to worker petitions. The Social Affairs Bureau summoned an inquiry yesterday and sent personnel to advise the workers. The details are recorded as follows:

Inquiry Process: Yesterday morning, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau summoned both labor and management for an inquiry. Ji Jiannan and Lao Huimin of Sanyou Industrial Society, Gong Yuting and Xia Zhongzhao of the 7th District Cotton Textile Industry Union, and Zhou Lianze of the Municipal Party Headquarters attended. Wang Xianqing of the Social Affairs Bureau presided, and Wang Zhiqin recorded. The chairman first reported, briefly stating that the case was being handled jointly by the Municipal Party Headquarters and the case had been submitted to the Municipal Government for arbitration. After instructions were received, they were ordered to reconcile again, so both parties were summoned again, hoping to resolve the matter as soon as possible with the principle of settling matters peacefully. The management reported that a shareholders' meeting was held yesterday and after repeated discussions, it was believed that there was a backlog of inventory, difficulties in economic circulation, and this year's market was not as good as last year, so there was no capacity to start work. The labor representatives reported that they had made concessions several times and hoped to resolve the matter as soon as possible, but the company made a profit last year, which is a fact. Now, instead of reducing the Hangzhou factory established in 1918, it is shifting responsibility to the general factory established in 1912, which is not justified legally or logically. Then the discussion began. The management requested to stop the workers from petitioning at the retail store to maintain business and refused to provide food expenses to the workers again. The labor representatives said that the workers' petition was spontaneous and a last resort. Later, the chairman proposed: (1) both labor and management should wait for the government to resolve the matter, (2) the management should maintain the workers' food expenses as usual, and (3) the labor representatives should be responsible for persuading the workers not to petition at the retail store again, hindering labor. Both parties were ordered to comply, and the meeting adjourned at 1:00 PM.

Sending Personnel to Advise: Xu Yefu, Head of the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, dispatched Zhu Jin together with Gong Yuting, Director of the 7th District Cotton Textile Industry Union, and others to the general factory of Sanyou Industrial Society in Yinxiang Township at 2:00 PM yesterday to advise all workers to wait for the Party and government authorities to resolve the matter according to law, and the food expenses will be provided by the management as usual, and the workers should no longer petition at the retail store, hindering business. The workers accepted the advice. It is reported that the Nanjing Road retail store of Sanyou Industrial Society is scheduled to resume business starting this morning.

Dafeng Factory Workers Resume Work Today 153

Labor-Management Dispute Awaiting Authorities to Mediate

Arrested Workers to Be Interrogated by the Court Today

After the labor unrest occurred at the Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory in West Shanghai, the court scheduled an interrogation today regarding the worker-police clash. The union resolved to resume work this morning, and the Party and government authorities thoroughly investigated yesterday. The Social Affairs Bureau scheduled mediation for today. The details are recorded as follows:

Party and Government Thorough Investigation: The Social Affairs Bureau, following instructions from the Municipal Government, properly handled the labor-management dispute at the Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, and dispatched Zhu Guilin together with Zhou Lianze of the Municipal Party Headquarters to the Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory of the 2nd District Dyeing Industry Union and the 6th District Police Station of the Public Security Bureau at 2:00 PM yesterday to thoroughly investigate the truth in order to mediate according to law.

Court Interrogation: The fifteen arrested workers, including Huang Guifen, were transferred to the Local Court by the Public Security Bureau for obstructing official duties, and a public prosecution will be filed. A hearing was specifically scheduled for 10:00 AM today. Yesterday, workers Feng Aming and Jiang Cairong, patrolman Hu Lizhong, and police officers Zhang Chuanfu, Sun Depu, and Zhu Hongbin were summoned to court for questioning.

Notice to Resume Work: The 3rd District Dyeing Industry Union issued a notice to all members yesterday stating that due to the unemployment of unemployed workers at the Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, there was no hope of resuming work, resulting in a complete cessation of work. Now, in order to maintain the livelihood of workers currently employed by the union, a meeting of directors was specifically convened and it was resolved to strongly advise workers currently employed to resume normal work, and strictly comply. This notice is hereby given. Acting Permanent Director Yu Ying, July 19, 1932.

Female Physiognomist Wen Ying Assassinated 155

Her Mother Also Injured

Nothing More Than a Love Affair

One Suspect Has Been Arrested

A woman known as Madam Wen Ying, surnamed Yang, is a female physiognomist. She lived with her mother, Wu, at No. 89 Pingle Lane, Racecourse Road, in the Public Concession. Yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM, she was suddenly murdered in her home and stabbed to death on the spot. Wu was also injured. Afterwards, the Zhabei police station sent detectives to pursue the murderer, and a suspect has already been arrested and temporarily detained at the police station for interrogation. The circumstances of Wen Ying's death are recorded as follows: Wen Ying, surnamed Yang, was 18 years old and originally from Shaoxing. She used to study at the female physiognomist Ling Qing's place. In the past two years, the teacher and apprentice separated and made a living by physiognomy, renting a house in Pingle Lane, which was quite narrow. She only hired a small maid to answer the door. Yesterday morning, a man named Fan Ruibao went to Wen Ying's place to visit. After a while, a man named Chen went to talk to her. Chen left first, and Fan left later. Around 3:50 PM, when Wen Ying was smoking opium on the couch, Fan suddenly came again and asked her to go to Lao Si's place. The woman refused, saying that if there was anything, Lao Si could be told to come and talk. Hu went. At this time, Wen Ying had gotten up and was dressing up at the dressing table. Her mother, Wu, was doing needlework next to her. Seeing that the woman was displeased, Fan took out a small silver coin from his pocket and gave it to the maid, A Jin, to buy cigarettes. The maid went out. About six or seven minutes later, because the small silver coin was made of lead, she dejectedly returned. When she reached the intersection of Second Malu and Xizang Road, she suddenly saw her mistress, Wu, running west with her clothes stained with blood, as if she was chasing someone. A Jin stepped forward to ask what was wrong, but she did not answer. So she returned home alone. Entering through the back door, she passed the stove shed and saw Wen Ying lying face down in the alley, covered in blood. She was greatly shocked and immediately reported to the patrolling police, who took Wen Ying and Wu to the hospital. Wen Ying died due to her serious injuries and could not be saved. She had three stab wounds on her body, one in the throat, one in the heart, and one in the left chest, all of which were fatal. Wu, 54 years old, had seven or eight wounds on her shoulders and hands, and her condition was also critical. It is reported that the deceased had an affair with the physiognomist Diao Keke, who lived in the New World, and later had a relationship with Fan Ruibao, the murderer. As for the man named Chen, it is said that he was also the woman's lover. Therefore, Wen Ying's death was nothing more than a love affair. The suspect arrested by the police was arrested from the New World Hotel.

Yellow Cattle Kneels and Bellows 156

Even Shed Tears and Escapes Death

Yesterday afternoon, at the intersection of Caishen Road and Laozha Road in the French Concession, a cattle dealer led nine yellow cattle through the area, intending to send them to the slaughterhouse on Titoni Lane. One of the cattle refused to move forward. The cattle dealer whipped it repeatedly, but it was still difficult to move it. Therefore, the other eight cattle were taken away first, and this cattle was left tied to a telephone pole on the side of the road. Unexpectedly, as soon as the cattle dealer left, the cattle broke the rope and rushed around, overturning several rickshaws along the way. Many people gathered to watch. After fleeing for a long time, it first entered the Si Ru Chun Noodle Restaurant and escaped from the back door, breaking into No. 177 Yanshou Lane, which is the accounting room of the Zhonghua Fuji Knitting Factory, which moved in this morning. No matter how much they shouted to drive it away, it would not leave, and the cattle knelt on the ground and bellowed. At this time, the cattle dealer also arrived and entered the factory to pull the cattle away. The manager of the factory, Qian, negotiated with the cattle dealer, saying that the factory had just moved in today, and the cattle rushing in was unlucky. Incense and candles must be prepared before it can be taken away. At that time, the cattle dealer misunderstood and called the Vietnamese police, reporting to the police station that the factory was detaining the cattle. After the police chief sent a detective to investigate, he realized it was a misunderstanding. Witnesses said that the cattle knelt on the ground and bellowed, and there were tear marks. Therefore, the factory manager negotiated with the cattle dealer and the factory paid $24.50 to buy the cattle and send it to the Release Life Bureau for raising and releasing.

The National Salvation Association telegraphed: Since the September 18th Incident, patriotic people have been running around calling for action and encouraging each other to strengthen their national spirit and prepare for a long-term resistance. Government authorities have repeatedly declared and encouraged the people to revive the national spirit and prepare for a long-term resistance. How can the words still be ringing in our ears, and the foreign troubles are getting deeper, but suddenly there is this self-destructive policy of public sale of opium. Recently, Wang Jingwei, Song Ziwen, Liu Ruiheng, and others have been running between Beijing, Shanghai, and Wuhan, secretly negotiating and about to turn the plan into a reality. At the same time, there are rumors in Jiangsu Province of dividing the area for tax package, and there is also a resolution in Hubei Province to cancel the ban on smoking opium by order. This is the proof. The main reason for the decline of the nation is the oppression of foreign troubles, and the harm of opium is known to all. The government has solemnly announced it as a strict prohibition for more than a day. At a time when the enemy is deep and things are urgent, efforts should be made to prohibit it, and there is no reason to impose prohibition on taxation. What's more, the government authorities' goal is not prohibition but taxation. If the public sale is not enough, they will continue to encourage planting and sales. If the encouragement of planting and sales is not enough, they will continue to force planting and sales. Eventually, the people under the blue sky and white sun will be reduced to blacklisted opium addicts. Then our Chinese nation will not wait for the iron hooves of the imperialists to destroy it, but will enter the tomb on its own. Moreover, in the past, we had an obligation to abide by the opium treaty between China and Britain, and we were also a signatory country to the Hague Convention on Prohibition of Opium. Whenever foreigners come to China for investigation, the government still covers up in every possible way. Now that it is once implemented for public sale, what will the international community think of us? Moreover, the so-called opium public sale system is a harsh policy of the British and Dutch countries towards their colonies. Japan will use it to destroy the Taiwanese nation. Now, the government authorities will definitely regard our people as slaves of a fallen country, but how do our people regard themselves? Now, let's take a hundred steps back. The reason why the government must carry out the public sale of opium is to save the poverty of finance. The economic panic in various countries in the world has reached its extreme. I have never heard of poisonous substances that harm the people being listed as a source of tax. It goes without saying that the current government authorities cannot bear to treat the people as grass and use harsh policies. With the arrogance of the military personnel in various provinces today, and the corruption of tax collection personnel, how can the so-called central government, which cannot command the country, hope to have a trickle of money go to the public? Just look at the provinces of Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Shaanxi, Hubei, Anhui, Henan, etc. Opium has been publicly sold for a long time. How much has it benefited the national treasury or the provincial treasury? In the past, the Qing Dynasty created Likin, which was also aimed at alleviating the urgent need for finance, and it has harmed us for decades. Now the government has decisively abolished it, and the disaster of public sale of opium is not a thousand times worse. Even if the government does not consider the rise and fall of the country, does it not consider the future generations? Our association, fearing the danger of drinking poison to quench thirst, and thinking about the danger of national subjugation and species extinction, hereby represents the 3 million people of Shanghai, vowing to oppose it to the death. I hope that compatriots across the country will rise up together to promote the government's reflection. I hereby telegraph to report, please be informed. Shanghai National Salvation Association

Wang Renlin Goes North to Investigate the Situation of Northern Laborers 163

Wang Renlin, acting director of the China branch of the International Labour Office, departed from Shanghai yesterday by train to head north, to investigate the situation of northern laborers, contact local organizations and scholars researching labor issues, and thereby seek to unify the organizations and work studying labor issues in China. It is said that this trip will last for one month, with stops in Nanjing, Jinan, Tianjin, and Beiping. While in Beijing, he will also liaise with the Ministry of Industry, requesting the National Government to approve the following international conventions as soon as possible: (1) establishing free public employment agencies; (2) female industrial and commercial workers should not work for six weeks before and after childbirth, and their salaries should be paid as usual; (3) child labor under the age of fourteen should not be engaged in industrial work; (4) agricultural workers should have the right to freely associate and assemble, equal to industrial workers; (5) industrial workers should have one day of rest each week; (6) workers should receive compensation for work-related injuries; (7) workers should receive disease compensation for work-related illnesses. The benefits given to laborers in the above seven labor conventions have all been recognized by our government and are included in various labor laws, so granting approval is merely a formality, which will not hinder the development of our industry and will at the same time win international goodwill.

Second Branch of the High Court Releases Pardoned Prisoners 164

The Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court recently received instructions from the Ministry of Judicial Administration to handle the amnesty. The amnesty procedure is roughly divided into three classes: (1) those sentenced to death, life imprisonment, or imprisonment for more than seven years will have one-third of their sentence commuted; (2) those sentenced to imprisonment for more than three years but less than seven years will have two-thirds of their sentence commuted; (3) those sentenced to imprisonment for less than three years will be completely pardoned. The branch court relayed the order to the First Special District Local Court under its jurisdiction, instructing it to gather all relevant files of those eligible for amnesty, categorize them by sentence length, and submit a list for review. However, due to the large number of files in the First Special Court, the review process will take some time, so they are starting with the files of those sentenced to imprisonment for less than three years. This has now been largely completed and reported to the High Branch Court, which reviewed and found twelve people eligible for amnesty last Saturday. Release warrants were immediately signed and sent to the prison warden for release. As of yesterday morning, three more people were found to be eligible for amnesty and were immediately brought to court, where Judge Yu announced their release in court. However, one of them was convicted of a crime of disturbing public morals, so he was ordered to provide bail as a restriction. It is reported that as of March 5, the First Special Court had sentenced more than two thousand criminals to imprisonment for less than three years. If all of them meet the amnesty regulations and are pardoned, the Tilanqiao Prison will be alleviated of overcrowding.
