The current Industrial and Commercial Trade Guild Law states that whether or not to join the guild is entirely up to the individual. As a result, the organization of trade guilds in various places cannot be soundly achieved. Those who join the guild are bound by the guild's articles of association and regulations, while those who do not join are free to operate, arbitrarily drop prices, and disrupt trade regulations. The guild is hindered by laws and cannot impose sanctions, so members of the guild are harmed. They will inevitably withdraw on the pretext of leaving, and the guild will disintegrate as a result. Therefore, the existence of trade guilds in name only is actually caused by the laws. The industry is extremely concerned. We are specially telephoning to request your consideration of the actual situation of industry and commerce and to amend the current Trade Guild Law as soon as possible. All businesses in any place that already have a trade guild organization should be required to join the trade guild as members, just as the Chamber of Commerce Law stipulates that trade guilds must join the Chamber of Commerce as members. This way, industrial and commercial products will not compete by arbitrarily dropping prices, but will seek progress by improving manufacturing technology. Otherwise, the collapse of industry and commerce will be imminent. If your lordships are concerned that the amendment of these regulations may lead to manipulation and monopoly by a few, then the local主管官廳, the highest party headquarters, and the superior chamber of commerce should be given as much close supervision and guidance as possible, and there will be no possibility of manipulation and monopoly. This telegraph is in urgent need of your attention and orders. (omitted below)

Public Security Bureau Interrogates Reactionaries Yesterday 174

According to Hua Dong She, at 7:30 on Saturday morning, a large number of young men and women were holding a Congress of Representatives from various districts of the Jiangsu County Communist Party in the Gonghe Theater at the intersection of Rue Robert and Jiaozhou Road in Western Shanghai, planning for the Eighth International Red Memorial Day and participating in riots. The Sixth District discovered the meeting and the director, Zhang Mingqin, sent police to surround the building and arrest everyone. Because the case was serious, after a brief interrogation of the ninety-two people, they were transported to the headquarters in three large trucks, where Director Wen ordered the Third Section to handle the case. Here is an exploration of the interrogation yesterday:

The Investigation Is Still Underway. According to a gentleman from the Second Section speaking to Hua Dong She reporters, this case is of great importance. Although many perpetrators have been apprehended, there are still a considerable number of hidden and uncaptured people. Therefore, although the case has been interrogated for two days and there are some clues, it is still necessary to protect the progress of the case in order to investigate the remaining perpetrators to suppress the emerging chaos. The perpetrators are currently sitting under the shade of the trees in the outer courtyard of the Third Section. There are a total of thirty-four people dressed as short-sleeved workers, guarded by six police officers. They are summoned into the room for individual interrogation. Due to the heat and the large number of people, only half of them have been questioned from morning to 4 PM, and the interrogation will continue today.

Further Evidence Obtained. When the perpetrators were arrested, various reactionary publications and red badges were found on their bodies. Yesterday, after a more detailed inspection, action diaries and secret code telegram books, C·P· passwords, etc. were found. The Public Security Bureau is currently studying these items in detail.

Postponement of Transfer. Yesterday, the perpetrators in the case were scheduled to be transferred by armed police officers to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for handling. However, according to Wu Zhiqian, the chief of the Third Section of the bureau, this case is a political crime, and the conditions of martial law and special conditions of the Communist Party should be handled by the garrison headquarters. However, because the interrogation has not yet been completed and the case involves many people and many keys, the transfer is postponed. After continuing to apprehend key individuals, the cases will be handled together.

Bail Not Allowed. Zheng Fuzhen, the owner of the Gonghe Theater, was also arrested because he allowed the Communist Party to hold a meeting. The family claimed that he was innocent and unknowingly harmed, and united with nearby businesses to request bail. However, the Public Security Bureau believes that the case has not been fully interrogated. Although it has been proven that Zheng is a law-abiding merchant, he should also be punished for benefiting from stupidity. Therefore, bail is not allowed until the whole case is clear. However, for the sake of consideration, he is being held in a separate room and treated with courtesy.

Advocate Strict Handling. Hua Dong She reporters interviewed Wen Yingxing, the director of the Public Security Bureau, yesterday morning and asked about the case. He said that since the beginning of the month, labor strikes have occurred frequently in this port. Although this is a result of the post-war social abnormality, it has caused disputes between labor and capital. It is not without the Communist Party's instigation, which has made the already devastated situation even more chaotic in order to achieve their conspiracy. Now that the August 1st Festival is approaching, the reactionaries have been thinking about making progress for a long time. The people who have been apprehended have all been found to be the backbone of the Communist Party, who incite labor movements. Therefore, I am very pleased with this case, because the apprehension of a large number of perpetrators can eliminate many sources of chaos in public security. Therefore, because the number of people involved is large, the interrogation is being carried out in detail, and it has been decided to deal with it strictly.

Feeling for Mussels, Feeling for a Corpse 175

Yang Fulang Killed During the War

The Corpse Still Hasn't Rotted After Nearly Half a Year

Yang Fulang, a resident of Yangjiazhai on the south bank of the Wenzaobang in Wusong, who is nearly sixty years old and makes a living by rowing a boat, on the second day of the lunar new year this year, the Japanese army planned to attack across the Wenzaobang with heavy troops in an attempt to occupy Wusong and were repelled by our army. The two sides fought fiercely in this battle, and bullets flew horizontally, as dense as raindrops. Yangjiazhai was right in the line of fire, so Yang Fulang dared not stay at home and fled from the hail of bullets to avoid danger. Unexpectedly, he was hit by two stray bullets. At that time, Yang still endured the pain and fled westward, but before he had gone far, he was exhausted and fell into the river and died. The body has not yet been recovered. The night before last, someone from the countryside was touching mussels by the bank of the river near Daxia Lane, west of the Yong'an Yarn Factory, when he touched a male corpse. The skin and flesh of the whole body had not rotted, but the clothes had been taken off long ago. Later, acquaintances identified the corpse as Yang Fulang's corpse and reported it to his son, Yang Ada, who went to identify it and confirmed it to be true. Therefore, yesterday morning, he prepared a coffin and collected the body.

The Inspection of Su Youxi's Tragic Death 177

Su Youxi, the Shanghai representative of the Northeast National Salvation Army from Beijing, was thirty-three years old. At around 9 AM on the morning of the day before yesterday, he was riding in his own car number 7267, driven by the driver Zheng Mulin, from west to east, passing through Hart Road. At that time, a tram number 68 from Route 1 was coming from the east. The driver Bao Ali was unable to react in time, and the two vehicles collided, causing the car to be largely damaged. Su and the driver were both seriously injured. A Chinese policeman number 439 saw the accident and immediately reported it to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, which ordered detectives to investigate. The two injured people were then sent to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment. Su died from his injuries at 5 PM that afternoon. The body was taken to the autopsy center on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court was notified and assigned prosecutor Guo Wei to come to the center to inspect the body. After taking his seat, he questioned Bao Ali, the driver of the tram, who said that he was thirty-four years old, from Suzhou, and lived at No. 26 Aiwen Lane, Hart Road. On that day, I was driving to Hart Road and saw two cars coming from the opposite direction, one behind the other. The car that caused the accident was originally in the back and wanted to overtake the car in front, so it accelerated and collided with my car. I was not driving fast at the time. After hearing a statement from Su's friend Liu Houwu, Guo determined that the deceased Su Youxi had indeed been injured and killed by tram number 68 from Route 2 before his death. The body was handed over to the friend Liu Houwu with a receipt to take back for burial.

Record of the Jiufu Company Shareholders' Meeting 178

The Jiufu Pharmaceutical Co., Ltd. held a shareholders' meeting the other day on the second floor of the company on Buck Road. The shareholders who attended the meeting were very enthusiastic. First, there was the unprecedented flood, then the fall of the Northeast, and then the fall in the price of local products in Southeast Asia. The market was depressed and the financial system was blocked. Domestic businesses were almost all declining and shrinking. The company worked hard and, under the reform of business policies, the sales of various products have shown significant progress, which is very gratifying. Then, supervisor Li Zhengfu reported on the accounts and distribution of surplus. Then, the chairman reported on the new factory construction plan, saying that the company's products, such as Bainianji, Shengdan, Jiufu cod liver oil emulsion, and Buliduo, have been welcomed by people at home and abroad. The factory director, chemist Shen Chuanhua, was asked to explain the plan for the construction of the new factory and the phased implementation plan for increasing production. It was approved by the shareholders, and the resolutions were passed. After the ad hoc discussion of several cases, the second supervisor was re-elected according to regulations. Ge Yanheng, Li Zhengfu, and Lu Mutang were still the most numerous and were re-elected, and Li Yipeng was the alternate supervisor.

Report on Reserve Fund Issue by the Four Banks 186

133rd Issue

The Four Banks Reserve Fund is jointly established by the Yanye, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu Banks to handle matters related to the issuance of banknotes by the Zhongnan Bank. According to the fund's issuance regulations, banknotes are issued with a full reserve. The cash reserve must be at least 60%, and the guarantee reserve must be at most 40%. A public announcement is made every week, and it is audited by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The following is a transcript of the 133rd announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Fund on July 16, 1932. The amount of banknotes in circulation is 18,863,157 yuan. The total amount of reserve funds is 18,863,157 yuan, including 11,621,426.87 yuan in cash reserve and 7,241,730.13 yuan in guarantee reserve.

Letters to the Editor

A Humble Opinion on the Abolition of Taels and the Change to Yuan (Continued) Wu Jing Xiong 195

Those who believe that the present is the best time to abolish taels and change to yuan think that the recent sharp drop in foreign silver dollars to 6 dimes and 9 cents means that people who receive silver dollars have invisibly reduced their income by 9%. Why not take this opportunity to abolish silver taels and set a standard conversion price of 7 dimes? If we don't act now, it will be difficult to implement it if the price of silver dollars rises again in the future (see the paper published by Mr. Zhang Naiqi in the "Current Affairs News" on July 12). This is certainly not wrong, but we must know that people who receive silver dollars have already reduced their income by 9% due to the sharp drop in the price of silver dollars. How much will it help to set a conversion price of 7 dimes to help them? If it is said that it prevents the price of silver dollars from falling further, then protection is added, but the current price of silver dollars and the actual value of silver coins are almost the same. If it falls further, silver smelters will be profitable and will compete to buy and melt it into silver bullion. Therefore, no matter what, the price of silver dollars will never fall below the actual value. This can be asserted, so why worry? According to the fact that the lowest price of silver dollars in the past could stand above 7 dimes, it was because the quality of silver coins at that time was better. For example, the actual value of foreign silver dollars was around 7 dimes and 1.5 cents, and foreign silver dollars were also outside of 7 dimes. When it came to Yuan coins in the third year of the Republic of China, the quality had already declined, but it was still worth above 6 dimes and 9 cents, so the price of silver dollars never broke the 7-dime barrier. In recent years, the number of coins minted by President Yuan has increased and the circulation has become wider, and almost all of the new coins are used in the market. However, the actual value is only about 6 dimes and 8.5 cents. The sharp drop in the price of silver dollars in the past six months, although it can be said to be due to economic decline, the difference in the quality of silver coins in the past and present is also an important reason. If we say that it is easier to set the conversion price at this low price of silver dollars, how can it be fair? The regulation of the conversion price must at least average the price of silver dollars in the most recent ten years, and then the compromise regulation can make the creditors and debtors no partiality to speak of, and the result of abolishing taels and changing to yuan is that the price of goods will rise, the cost of living will increase, and society will be seriously affected. We do not mean that society should not endure this temporary pain, but at a time when production is declining and all industries are in recession, there is no time to recuperate, so how can we give it a strong laxative? Is this the best time?

In short, the abolition of taels and the change to yuan are beyond reproach, and it is almost as unshakable as Einstein's theory of relativity. The gold standard of the Gammer Plan is unattainable. To retreat and think about the next best thing, the abolition of taels and the change to yuan is also enough to establish the foundation for improving the monetary system. Therefore, we strongly advocate the abolition of taels and the change to yuan, and we hope to see it come true as soon as possible. However, looking ahead and behind, there are many obstacles. If we are not careful, hundreds of coins will be created, causing endless harm. Therefore, we advocate that before the abolition of taels and the change to yuan, at least the following prerequisites must be met:

(1) Use diplomatic and legal methods to prohibit foreign merchants' banks from issuing banknotes.

(2) Unify the national issuing rights and stipulate full reserves (such as the Hong Kong government's method) and closely supervise them.

(3) Centralize the minting rights, determine the weight, quality, and free minting of the new standard currency, and ensure accurate quality.

(4) Compromise and regulate the conversion price of taels and yuan, so as to be impartial.

If the above four issues can be resolved one by one, then the abolition of taels and the change to yuan will naturally reach a stage where everything is ready and success is halfway there, and what could be better than this? Otherwise, a hasty attempt to achieve success will be counterproductive and will only lead to resentment. Moreover, if we suddenly announce the abolition of taels and the change to yuan today without any preparation, which of the dozens of hard and soft currencies will be used as the standard currency? Without first thoroughly reorganizing the national currency, how can we achieve the effect of abolishing taels and changing to yuan? If the weeds are not removed and the seeds are sown, it is difficult to get good harvests. Fellow citizens, please think about this!

Free Talk

Talks on the Second Floor

Wonderful Yu Ruolan 196

— Zhan Lu

The puppet state sent a maiden petition group to the east to request recognition. The team leader is called Yu Ruolan! Since it is a Han surname, she must be a Han Chinese girl. Why did she become a representative of the puppet state? When I read the newspaper to this point, I said, "Wonderful, Yu Ruolan!"

Someone said: "This is not wonderful at all. What's so wonderful about it?" I said, "The matter is not wonderful at all, but the name is wonderful—only because the two words 'maiden' make up the word 'wonderful.'" Wonderful Yu Ruolan! Poetry comes all at once:

Wonderful! Wonderful! My surname is Yu, my name is Ruolan!

As a Han Chinese woman, she went over the wall! Women do the sides, —"West Chamber" becomes a female traitor, went to the eastern three islands to play!

Play, play, don't care if the graves of seventeen or eighteen generations of ancestors have collapsed.

Wonderful! Wonderful! Leading a maiden group!

Holding the geta under the dwarf's feet, shouting "Long live under your feet, long live under your feet!"

Recognize the Kwantung puppet state as an independent country in name as soon as possible!

Let those geta come and go alone!

Never again allow the one whose surname is Feng to occupy the sea, the one whose surname is Ma to occupy the mountain.

Wonderful! Wonderful! The maiden leader, a sprig of orchid!

Neither Hua Mulan who joined the army in place of her father, nor Su Ruolan who wove a celestial brocade!

Just a stinking flower, —a grass name

Impersonating a fragrant orchid.

Neither a valley orchid nor a nine-mu orchid!

This orchid, could it have grown on Pig Head Mountain?

Even if it didn't grow on Pig Head Mountain, it should have grown on a dung heap!

I call you, Yu, Ruolan!

I sigh for you, Alas! Ruolan!

The Flower Spear Money 197

— Ding Ming

When Mr. Wang Xingbo was about to leave for Suzhou, he told me the story of his martial arts teacher, Mr. Qian Wenming, who was known as "Flower Spear Money." After listening to it, I felt it was very strange, and now I am sweating and writing it out.

Native Place and Alias: Flower Spear Qian is from Qianjia Village in Zhenjiang. Because he used a good flower spear technique, and when he wielded it, it was as long as silk, as round as a full moon, and no wind or rain could leak through his body, others gave him the nickname "Flower Spear Qian."

Characteristics of Boxing Skills: Flower Spear Qian's boxing technique is of the Fu school; the characteristic of this boxing technique is that it is neither rigid nor soft. It does not have the two major drawbacks of the Shaolin school being too rigid and high-pressure, nor the Tai Chi school being too soft and without resistance; the wonderful part of the spear technique lies in the flexibility of the grasping of the yin and yang hands, and the strength is exerted in an instant without any effort.

Appearance and Anecdotes: Flower Spear Qian is tall and thin, slovenly, and walks as weakly as a patient. He often carries a three-foot-long copper-headed, steel-boned pipe; but on the outside of the pipe, there are densely twisted black silk threads; when he smokes, he only uses his mouth to slant and hold it without any effort, just like a wooden pipe. Therefore, in the eyes of a third party, he is just an ordinary weakling! But when something happens, he becomes as brave as a living dragon and tiger, and the pipe also becomes his protective weapon at the same time.

Appetite: Flower Spear Qian eats three liters of rice and two chickens and ducks per meal. His appetite is really big! Fifteen years ago, Mr. Wang often invited him to dinner, and his appetite was ten times that of an average villager; one night, he came to Mr. Wang's house when Mr. Wang and his family were about to finish eating. He was asked to eat with them, and the old gentleman was unceremoniously sat at the table, ate the meals of more than ten female servants that night, and even ate the entire Wang family's breakfast the next day. In the end, he still said he wasn't full!

Behavior, Age, and Family Background: Mr. Wang has not heard from Flower Spear Qian for more than ten years; it is said that this old gentleman is a poor but unyielding and non-productive big glutton, living a wandering life every year; he rarely gets sick in his life, and if he is sick, he only needs to meditate for a while, and then he recovers! He is now about eighty-three years old; he has a son, a nephew, and a nephew, all of whom have considerable inheritance; among the three, his nephew is especially outstanding!

Thoughts: After hearing everything about Teacher Qian, I expressed my admiration and my spirit was indeed greatly inspired; my love for martial arts was also tense. However, it is a pity that an old gentleman like this did not broadly teach disciples, nor did he study science, nor did he understand the modern situation, and could not further contribute a little to society, oh! Even if he lived to be eight hundred and three years old, he would only pass through the world casually!

The Shoe King Bata 198

— Ma Juncao

Currently, the most famous "uncrowned king" in the industrial world

Naturally, it should be the American car king Ford. His thoughts, insights, and life have all been talked about. Here, I will introduce a European Ford - Bata, the shoe king of Czech Zlin. Bata's reputation in East Asia is not as loud as that of the Swedish match king Kreuger. But their unnatural deaths are the same. Bata's thoughts and opinions are exactly the same as Ford's. Their lives are also very similar.

Bata was born in the countryside of Czechoslovakia. His father was also a shoemaker. So he helped his father make shoes, deal with customers, and solicit business from an early age. At the age of eighteen (1894), he opened his own small-scale shoe store. But business was not very good. In 1904, he decided to go to the United States and France to learn new shoe-making and sales methods. After returning to China, he adopted Ford's mass production principles, increased efficiency, and reduced costs. In this way, his career became more prosperous day by day. During the European War, he specialized in making military leather shoes and earned a lot of money.

Bata has thirty-two shoe factories. Employing 17,600 workers. The daily output is 90,000 pairs of leather shoes. 40,000 pairs of rubber shoes. 4,000 pairs of bedroom slippers. Other special shoes 5,000 pairs. There are 1,946 issuing offices within the country. There are 153 abroad. The shoe market is not only all over Europe (except Soviet Russia). And as far away as the United States and Egypt. In addition to shoe factories, Bata also operates leather factories related to shoe manufacturing. Yarn factories. Textile factory. Rubber factories, etc. Therefore, the raw material cost of his products can be especially cheap.

The main reason for Bata's success. It is not the cheap raw materials. He pays special attention to the distribution of profits. Every worker is willing to take responsibility for himself. Because the distribution of profits is based on the work efficiency of each worker. Bata's treatment of workers. Just like Ford. There are free tutoring schools in the factory. Hospital. Movie theater. Dormitory. There are also cheap restaurants. Consumer society. Although the price of his leather shoes has dropped from an average of six yuan and six jiao to one yuan and five jiao. But workers' wages have tripled.

Bata's only hobby is aviation. He has many private planes. His use of airplanes. Just like ordinary wealthy people use cars. Five years ago, he was seriously injured when the wings caught fire and fell to the ground. If he had been safely inside this time. There would never have been four pieces of torn bodies. It can only be said that his fate was not good.

Talks from a Vegetarian Studio 201

— Gan Yi

Zhu Qinglan

The world knows Zhu Qinglan as a philanthropist. It is also known that Qinglan was a military general. He was indeed a modest and refined gentleman with the demeanor of a famous scholar. When waiting for a position in Shenyang, before it had been changed to a province and the name of Shengjing was still in use, the Qing court had stationed a general to govern affairs. After General Zengqi left, Zhao Erxun succeeded him. Erxun valued his talent and appointed Qinglan as the leader of the patrol army, later promoting him to commander. He was transferred to Jinzhou. He accumulated wealth up to the rank of Daoist Priest. Before the Russo-Japanese War, the area was near the sea, and many people gathered there to avoid the conflict. Good and bad elements were mixed, making public order a concern. Qinglan supervised his troops day and night, patrolling and executing bandits immediately, then reporting to the general. Erxun complained, "Why not seek orders first?" Qinglan replied, "A general abroad is not bound by the ruler's commands, let alone those of a superior. The matter is urgent and should not be delayed. Therefore, I acted according to circumstances. I have not wrongly killed a single person. If any innocent person has been killed, Qinglan is willing to accept the consequences." Erxun said, "Just ensure that is the case, or I will hold you responsible." As a result, the territory under his jurisdiction was peaceful. Later, when Erxun supervised Sichuan, he recommended Qinglan as a commander, equivalent to today's division commander. During the Xinhai Revolution in Sichuan, Erxun's brother, Erfeng, was the governor and arrested and persecuted party members. Qinglan disagreed and requested to leave. A powerful figure in Sichuan, Yin Changheng, raised troops and killed Erfeng. Qinglan then left Sichuan under pretense and entered the Republic of China. Erxun praised him as more virtuous than the president and appointed him as the governor of Heilongjiang. His political achievements were remarkable. He retired, then returned to office as the governor of Guangdong Province. When the Southwest declared independence, he was not tolerated by the military governor Chen and resigned. Having served in Jinzhou for a long time, he settled there. In recent years, he traveled to several provinces, organizing disaster relief and saving people, rarely finding a moment of peace. The world views him as a philanthropist, and it is fitting without shame.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Speech

A View of Life: To Die Under a Peony 202

— Buddha

In this complex and chaotic social state, views on life are extremely diverse. Some see getting promoted and becoming wealthy as the purpose of life; others see gambling and eating as the purpose of life; some see becoming a hero as the purpose of life; some see becoming a famous scholar as the purpose of life; some see flattering as the purpose of life. In general, it can be said that each person has their own view of life, and there is no fixed definition. The ancient saying, "To die under a peony, to be a ghost and still be romantic," was originally a witty and satirical remark. However, in today's society, there are those who have created a new perspective, taking "To die under a peony, to be a ghost and still be romantic" as their view of life, which is truly a wonder of the world.

Recently, newspapers have reported numerous cases of couples dying together in the Huangpu River or in hotels. It is truly passion to the extreme, passion even to death, continuing the passion after death. It is as if people are born with no other purpose than to "write love letters" and "talk sweet nothings," solely for the sake of "opening a company" and "sexual desire." Their entire lives are sacrificed for passion. The so-called "To die under a peony, to be a ghost and still be romantic" is truly astonishing. Just as yesterday's newspaper reported, the water police found the bodies of a young man and woman at the No. 16 buoy, embracing each other, with a belt tying them together. It was clearly a suicide due to lost love. The man was named Ruan Chengxun, and the woman was named Xu Juying, which is one example.

However, the use of "qing" (情, emotion/love) is broad. For example, parents loving their children is qing, and children being filial to their parents is also qing. Extending this to brothers, sisters, relatives, and friends, mutual affection is all qing. Does the meaning of qing only exist in these ways, and is there no qing outside of this? If that is truly the case, then the many, many lovers on the Fourth Road and on the Ni'ni Ying Road would all go to the Huangpu River to die, truly dying in droves. The ancients said, "To love is to want them to live, to hate is to want them to die." Now, they are doing the opposite, loving and wanting them to die. Does that mean hating and wanting them to live? Truly, people's hearts have changed greatly, greatly changed.

During the Warring States period, Queen Dowager Xuan of Qin had an affair with Wei Choufu. When the Queen Dowager was about to die, she issued an order: "When I am buried, Wei Choufu must be buried with me as a sacrifice." Wei Choufu was troubled by this. Someone persuaded the Queen Dowager for Wei Choufu, saying, "Do the dead have knowledge?" The Queen Dowager said, "No, they do not." The person said, "Your Majesty's spirit clearly knows that the dead have no knowledge. Why bury the one you love in life with a dead person who has no knowledge? If the dead had knowledge, the late king would have accumulated anger for a long time. How could he have had time for his affair with Wei Choufu?" The Queen Dowager then stopped the order. This story clearly shows that if one truly loves someone, one would never want them to die in vain. Even though Queen Dowager Xuan was licentious, she was still able to realize this.

To be even more straightforward, life is inherently empty, and death will come one day. If one must die anyway, there are many ways to die. For example, Jing Ke and Nie Zheng dying as assassins is one way to die. Tian Heng and Wen Tianxiang refusing to be slaves of a conquered nation is also a way to die. Xu Xilin, Xiong Chengji, Tang Caichang, and the seventy-two martyrs of Huanghuagang dying for the revolution is also a way to die. Similarly, the soldiers who bravely resisted Japan this time and the righteous volunteers of the Northeast are also dying in a way. Like the Americans who flew around the world in eight days, and now someone wants to fly around the world in six days, that is also a way to die. All are sacrifices, all are deaths, but one is a death of great integrity, while the other is a death of filth and squalor, truly as different as Mount Tai and a feather.

The only problem people have is being greedy for life and fearing death. If one is not afraid of death, there is always a way. Therefore, sacrifice is not impossible, but it must be worthwhile and meaningful. Even the great heroes of the past were merely not afraid of death. If one dies simply for a woman, dies helplessly, it is truly foolish and useless.

Due to business, I traveled south to Fujian and accepted an invitation from Mr. Lin Shouchang. Last night, I traveled from Beijing to Shanghai by train, passing through Kunshan and Nanxiang. Leaning against the window, I surveyed the battlefield, the dark moon and sparse stars, and the desolate scenery. In the hazy moonlight, the scenery is desolate and overgrown with weeds; ruined fortresses and remaining bee hives, a few willows stand. The small grass faces the wind, as if mourning; the bloodstains of loyal souls gradually blur.

Who is the enemy? Who is the friend? Wounds have not healed, yet another journey begins. Three things remain in my heart: aging parents, impoverished people, and the cries of ghosts.

Science

Marsh Gas Lamp 205

— Yun

"Marsh gas" has been known since ancient times. It can be obtained from the edges of springs and ponds. The method is to stir up the sediment on the bottom of the water with a bamboo pole, causing many small bubbles to be released on the surface. These small bubbles are collected by inverting a glass cup over them. When the glass cup is lifted, quickly bring a flame to the mouth of the cup to ignite the gas, which will burn with a blue flame. This is the burning of marsh gas. It is now being used as a substitute for electric lights and fuel, known as natural gas lamps.

The chemical composition of marsh gas is methane. Its chemical formula is CH4. For experimental purposes, use about five grams of dry sodium acetate, mixed with an equal amount of sodium hydroxide and a small amount of lime powder. Heat the mixture in a hard test tube, and this gas will be produced. Its Western name is Methane. Because its two molecules are combustible, it produces a strong blue flame. Ordinary plant matter will also produce this gas when it rots in a place with insufficient air. The mud at the bottom of ponds also contains a large amount of decaying plants, so it will also produce this gas.

The method of using it to make natural gas lamps is to tightly seal vegetable leaves, rice bran, rice washing water, cow dung, etc., in an airtight underground cellar. Add clear water on top. After one or two weeks, the vegetable leaves, rice bran, etc., will rot and produce this marsh gas. Use a six-foot pole to stir it, allowing the gas to pass through an iron pipe. At the mouth of this iron pipe, place a safety lamp (i.e., a gauze-covered lamp) similar to a gas lamp to burn the gas, which can then be used as a substitute for electric lights. If the arrangement is changed to resemble the mouth of a pressure stove (different from a pressure stove in that one emits gas from a small tube and the other emits gas from multiple small tubes), then it can be used as a substitute for a pressure stove as fuel.

The burning of marsh gas can cause an explosion if it is carelessly mixed with air. Therefore, the installation of this natural gas lamp cannot be done carelessly.

Businesses engaged in this industry use cement cellars and measure the dimensions of the cellar, the amount of plant waste used, and calculate the amount of marsh gas that can be produced. They also specially manufacture a type of pressure gauge to measure it. The lamp head and iron pipe arrangements are all specially manufactured and sold after research.

There are many vegetable leaves, rice washing water, and other waste materials in the countryside. It is not easy to obtain them in the city. Therefore, this type of installation is suitable for the countryside. However, the cost of installing a cement cellar and iron pipe lamp head is very high. It is not easy for ordinary people in the countryside to afford such equipment, so it cannot yet compete with the power of electricity. Moreover, this type of installation has no secrets and cannot be patented. However, those who wish to install it should at least hire someone with knowledge of chemistry and craftsmanship to supervise the process, otherwise there may be danger or, even if there is no danger, it may not be economical. Caution is advised.

Epilogue

Sick Car 206

— Wu

The avenue is filled with people and cars: trams, horse-drawn carriages, rickshaws, carts, trucks, cars with white license plates, and cars with black license plates. Coming and going, horizontal and vertical, crowded and packed.

Suddenly, a car with a black license plate stopped, as if suffering from a sudden illness, unable to move. As a result, the cars behind had to stop as well, the first car, the second car, the third car, and so on. All had to stop. For a moment, the cars formed a dead dragon on the road. The tram was also stuck in the middle, ringing its bell incessantly.

Now, someone got out of the sick car with the sudden illness. The person was wearing a British-style suit, with trousers tapered to the extreme, yellow leather shoes, a stiff straw hat, and a mustache only two fingers wide below the nose. Based on these characteristics, we immediately knew that he was a citizen of the Great Empire. What was he doing? Of course, as usual, he checked the machinery. However, the sick car was not as easy to diagnose as he had hoped, so he became flustered. The road could not be blocked for even a moment, and the horns and bells behind him were ringing incessantly. Then, an Indian Sikh came, and onlookers also gathered. Of course, our Sikh could only shake his head. The only solution was to help the citizen of the Empire push the sick car to the side of the road so that the blocked cars could pass.

However, this was not the best solution, as the car could not just be left on the road, and he could not just stand there guarding it. He had to find a way to get it back. Finally, he had an idea. He called out to the idle people on the street, his Shanghai dialect so unskilled that it made people cringe.

"Hey, can a few of you come and push it back for me? I'll pay you."

But no one answered him. Everyone looked at him with a scornful smile and walked away. However, for the sake of money, someone finally asked him:

"How much will you pay each person?"

"To Gordon Road, two mao per person, okay?"

"Two jiao? From the avenue to Gordon Road? Bah!"

"Then how much do you want?"

"Five people, at least five yuan each, not a penny less!"

"Hahahaha!" Everyone burst into laughter.

"Foreigner, bad guy, ignore him," someone said.

"Hahahaha!" Another burst of laughter.

After people had a moment of laughter here, they soon walked away. Foreign devil, killer of Chinese people, bad guy. Who would pay attention to him? This was also a kind of revenge.

Live in Dreams, Die in Reality

Liva Lita Village 207

— Bei Lei

Like a carpet of fallen leaves, filled with the fragrance of flowers and fluttering shadows, with lingering music and elegant singing and dancing. Look! The wine is as fiery as fire, and the girls are as beautiful as flowers. Another world, a paradise on earth, this is the Shanghai High-Class Women's Summer Pleasure Gathering.

"High-class women," I don't qualify at all. I am just a low-class literary beggar. "Summer pleasure," is it necessary to eliminate the summer, and where does the pleasure come from? A silver dollar, like snow, menacingly guards the village gate. This is a gold-consuming place for capitalists and a place of wandering for the poor.

It was an extremely hot twilight. Yun came and insisted on inviting me to enjoy the scene. Suffering me, poor me, where would the money come from? What interest did I have in going? I refused, saying: The high-class women's pleasure gathering is definitely not a place for a poor scholar like me to go.

Yun was not angry. He said: Go, you must go, it is very interesting there, and there is a lady with the same name as you.

"Same name, really?"

"Who's lying to you?"

My curiosity was piqued. Finally, Yun paid the "toll" to enter. "Liang Garden is good, but it is not a place to stay for long." I don't know why, but when we poor fellows enter a place where the nobles gather and stand together, we always feel a little flustered. So, I was overwhelmed by their grandness.

Yes, the blue water rippled, and small boats swayed. The green trees were lush, truly a summer resort. How lively! How joyful! Men and women, in clusters, smiled with blooming faces.

Yun knew how to dance, so he went to the ballroom as soon as he entered the gate. He said that Mr. XX and Miss XX's tango was very exciting and should not be missed, and that the Miss with the same name as you could also be seen by the opportunity. Of course, if I didn't go with him, what would I do?

I had never been to a ballroom before. This time, I broadened my horizons.

Men, with lustful expressions on their faces, women, with grotesque and almost naked appearances, held each other tightly and danced madly. The smooth floor would make me unstable. Everyone was happy. The summer pleasure gathering lived up to its name.

I sat in the shade of a tree, looking around. I suddenly thought that less than half a year ago, this place, directly opposite, had the Toyota Textile Mill with enemy armored cars patrolling the area. My conscience made me ashamed. I discovered that everyone coming and going had lost all sense of morality. The Northeast was fighting so fiercely, but the people here with leisurely sentiments had forgotten everything.

I didn't want to watch anymore, so I ran away. I only realized that these people would only wake up after the country was destroyed. I deeply regretted coming here, but it was too late.

Nanjing Road at Night 208

— Xing

Standing on the high floor of a certain building, I overlooked Nanjing Road at night.

Although it is night, under the illumination of countless electric lights, it is not only as bright as day, but also more brilliant and radiant than daytime.

Huge buildings stand in rows, regularly and heavily, separated by a road facing each other. The huge shadows stretched across the center of the road, like a giant beast opening its massive mouth.

The flowing groups of cars, the crowded trams, and the masses of people flowed like water on the road. No one was without a tense expression and a fighting spirit, as if they had heard the sound of a charge, rushing forward in a hurried and urgent manner... crowding. This is "life," this is "human society."

Among the hurried and urgent crowd rushing forward, the "strong" and the "weak" are even more evident. The strong often have a proud smile on their faces, often open their greedy mouths to devour everything, and often widen their greedy eyes, waiting for the opponent in the struggle, chasing after the docile lambs. The weak can only struggle helplessly, or hide in dark corners, stealing the leftovers of the strong.

Electric lights emit various colors of light from various buildings, especially the "red" color, which is particularly dazzling. The great "red" color is a symbol of blood, a signal of struggle, planted like fire on the highest peak of Nanjing Road, which is made of blood and flesh, giving mankind a great revelation.

The noisy sounds, rising with the flow of people, include laughter, cries, wails, and also mixed with roars of anger.

In the corners of the road, there are many enchanting eyes flickering, and many lips painted with rouge are whispering. The trembling breasts and swaying fat hips are calling out, "Come on, come on!" These are seductive shouts, also shouts of life, the enchanting is mixed with endless sorrow and strong resentment!

The patrolmen with killing handguns hanging diagonally stood in the center of the intersection, stretching out their two fingers to direct the vehicles and the crowds. Obviously, the order of this society is built on top of force. I wondered if this force would one day be seized by another group of people........

The night grew deeper. The "crowded people" were all resting temporarily, preparing the strength for tomorrow's struggles and competitions. The bodies of the weak remained on both sides of the road. The wide and long road also exhaled a deep, bitter breath from the day's fatigue.

Family Problems

Conflict of Old and New Minds 209

— Kang Shi

To my neighbors, the old Mr. and Mrs. Zheng, are a natural good match. They have two sons, who are already married. They also have three daughters, the eldest of whom is already married. The second and third daughters have not yet married, but they are already past the age of sixteen.

The eldest son and daughter-in-law, although only thirty years old, are a retired couple from the trend of the times. Their most peculiar habit is that they don't like to talk all day long.

However, the second daughter is a good mover with a new mind. She has also read for a few years. Every Sunday, she always strolls in the park with her lover—her fiancé—and her fiancé comes to her home every day. Their love can be said to have reached the boiling point!

The old Mr. and Mrs. Zheng are a naturally good couple, so they let their daughter move freely and are good at adapting to the trend!

However, the eldest son and daughter-in-law are a couple who have fallen behind the times. Of course, they don't agree with their sister's behavior and sometimes raise objections.

Because of the difference between the old and new minds, they have different opinions and have had several conflicts.

I remember once, because of some small things, the sister-in-law and daughter-in-law, who already had different opinions, quarreled. Of course, in a fit of anger, everyone revealed their dirty secrets. The chopsticks and tea sets were sacrificed. The old Mr. Zheng was so angry that he couldn't speak. The old Mrs. Zheng happened to be back in her hometown of Lingnan for something, so a full-fledged brawl was finally dissuaded by an old Mrs. Sun next door. However, the people watching the excitement had already crowded the doorway, and from then on, the family scandal was spread.

Black Curtain

Black Curtain of Indian Black Coal 210

Black curtain events happen often, but in recent years, due to the high cost of living and the economic downturn, there are many black-hearted Indian black coals that are taking advantage of this opportunity to open their black curtain—lending companies—gathering unscrupulous followers to be communicators (i.e., commonly known as runners) to widely recruit debtors. Therefore, those who lack money, after hearing the sweet words of the runners, often join the debt group. However, once in the grip, Indian black coals use their usual tricks and procedures. The method is to deceive the borrowers into writing a fake IOU, writing one or two times more than the amount of money (this is a fixed procedure), writing the interest as one or half a cent, but in fact collecting eight or nine cents per month. At this time, the borrowers are half deceived by the Indian black coals and runners, and half oppressed by the economy. Although they know they are being deceived, they can only drink poison to quench their thirst and reluctantly write the note. When exchanging the silver dollars and the IOU, which differ by half the amount, the heavy interest for the first month is immediately deducted. The runner forcibly demands shoe money. In addition, this Indian man, using the qualification of creditor, often goes to the debtor's house to play, often engaging in various unscrupulous and lustful desires (such as rape, beating, scolding, demanding children, taking goods without giving money, claiming to increase interest, etc.). If the debtor dares to object, he immediately turns hostile and goes to the court to falsely accuse the debtor of not repaying the principal and interest, ignoring the guarantor, and using the fake IOU written out of helplessness at the time as a legitimate reason to request the court to recover the money. However, at this time, the debtor is like a patient who is terminally ill, unable to save himself or seek help, just like a terminally ill patient for whom even famous doctors are helpless. Is this not unjust? Those who have been deceived need not be remembered, but those who have not been deceived should pay attention.

Fragments of Summer Nights 211

— Wu

In order to eliminate the summer night heat, modern men and women embrace and drive cars on the road, opening their collars and baring their chests, almost with the feeling of "pleasant masculine wind." At the same time, on both sides of the same road, many broken men and women lie sprawled, recklessly exuding a very strong smell of sweat, so that modern men and women have to cover their noses and pass by, even cursing fiercely, saying, "Disgusting filthy things! They should die, they should die." But the broken men and women also wave their big fists and say, "......One day will come, and we will clean up these dog men and women!"

XXX 212

Night is deep, and the toiling people drag their heavy bodies to the basement to rest from their extreme fatigue, but the people above them, pressing down on them, are reveling and dancing. A burst of endless music mixed with heavy footsteps shocks their nerves, so that they are constantly disturbed and cannot sleep. So they roar, "Curse your mother! There will be a time when we will completely overturn the foundation, and see if you can still have fun!"

XXX 213

A rickshaw puller pulled a large man to the door, wiping his sweat while reaching out his hand to accept his hard-earned wages, and begging repeatedly to add a little more. Sure enough, the big man said generously, "Okay, because it's hot, I'll give you one more copper coin."

XXX 214

Mrs. Wang was playing cards. Because the weather was too hot, in addition to the large electric fan rotating above her head, she also ordered the maid to fan her from behind. This made her feel cool. So the maid was covered in sweat, while the wife was full of coolness. So the maid was plagued by sleep, while the wife was extremely energetic.

XXX 215

The clock had already struck two past noon, and A Gen was still shaking the ice cream, shaking it again and again. His arms had already been shaken so sore that he had to stop to rest and close his eyes. But unfortunately, he was discovered by the young master, who had just finished smoking his opium. He stamped his feet and cursed loudly, "Damn thing, others are waiting to eat, but you are sleeping. In such a hot night, do you think you can sleep without eating ice cream?"

Market News 216

Guanghua Printing Company specializes in printing bookkeeping books. Guanghua Printing Company in Ti Lan Qiao specializes in serving major banks and promoting new bookkeeping methods. Since its establishment, it has had an eight-year history. Its low prices, beautiful products, fast processing, and reliable deadlines have earned it a good reputation.
